Feature Name: Orders

Endpoint: GET /admin/orders
  OperationId: GetOrders
  Summary: List Orders
  Security: api_token, cookie_auth, jwt_token
  Query Parameters:
    - fields, in=query, type=string, optional
    - offset, in=query, type=number, optional
    - limit, in=query, type=number, optional
    - order, in=query, type=string, optional
    - id, in=query, type=oneOf, optional
    - status, in=query, type=oneOf, optional
    - $and, in=query, type=array, optional
    - $or, in=query, type=array, optional
    - sales_channel_id, in=query, type=array, optional
    - region_id, in=query, type=oneOf, optional
    - q, in=query, type=string, optional
    - created_at, in=query, type=object, optional
    - updated_at, in=query, type=object, optional
    - customer_id, in=query, type=oneOf, optional
    - with_deleted, in=query, type=boolean, optional
  Responses:

Endpoint: GET /admin/orders/{id}
  OperationId: GetOrdersId
  Summary: Get an Order
  Security: api_token, cookie_auth, jwt_token
  Path Parameters:
    - id, in=path, type=string, required
  Query Parameters:
    - fields, in=query, type=string, optional
    - id, in=query, type=oneOf, optional
    - status, in=query, type=oneOf, optional
    - version, in=query, type=number, optional
    - created_at, in=query, type=unknown, optional
    - updated_at, in=query, type=unknown, optional
    - deleted_at, in=query, type=unknown, optional
  Responses:
    - Status: 200 - OK
      Content-Type: application/json

Endpoint: POST /admin/orders/{id}/complete
  OperationId: PostOrdersIdComplete
  Summary: Complete Order
  Security: api_token, cookie_auth, jwt_token
  Path Parameters:
    - id, in=path, type=string, required
  Query Parameters:
    - fields, in=query, type=string, optional
  Request Body:
    Content-Type: application/json
    Model: postordersidcomplete_body
    Type: object
    Description: Pass additional custom data to the API route. This data is passed to the underlying workflow under the `additional_data` parameter.
    Properties:
  - additional_data: object, (optional)
  Responses:

      Content-Type: application/json
